  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{population =} \FunctionTok{recode}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      population,}
      \StringTok{"UNREL22"}  \OtherTok{=} \StringTok{"UNREL\_22"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{"UNREL120"} \OtherTok{=} \StringTok{"UNREL\_120"} \CommentTok{\#fix coding errors in data file: Two pops were inconsistently labelled.}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{Ci =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(cue }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"light"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{is\_evo =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(EE }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"ANC"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{evo\_type =} \FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      EE }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"ANC"}   \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{      EE }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"REL"}   \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{      EE }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"UNREL"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
      \ConstantTok{TRUE}          \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_integer\_}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{g\_chr =} \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(grandmother),}
    \AttributeTok{m\_chr =} \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(mother),}
    \AttributeTok{mat\_code =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(g\_chr, m\_chr),}
    \AttributeTok{mat\_id =} \FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      mat\_code }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"AN"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{      mat\_code }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"NN"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}

\NormalTok{      mat\_code }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"NA"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{4}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
      \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_integer\_}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{cue\_index =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(Ci }\SpecialCharTok{==} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{state\_id =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(mat\_id), }\DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L} \SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ (mat\_id }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ cue\_index, }\ConstantTok{NA\_integer\_}\NormalTok{),}

    \AttributeTok{block\_id =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(block))}

  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{EE\_seq\_chr =} \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(EE\_seq),}
    \AttributeTok{EE\_seq\_id =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(EE\_seq\_chr), }\DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(EE\_seq\_chr)))}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}

\NormalTok{  )}

      \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{any}\NormalTok{(evo\_type }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ pop\_rel\_id }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\&}
      \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{any}\NormalTok{(evo\_type }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ pop\_unrel\_id }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}

A series of sanity checks, if any of these don't check out then our data
processing has gone off the rails.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Ci }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{mat\_id }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{state\_id }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{is\_evo }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{evo\_type }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{)))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{block\_id }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{EE\_seq\_id }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pop\_rel\_id }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{))}
\FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pop\_unrel\_id }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{0}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Setup the stan data, basically we need a named list with each piece of
data that will get passed to stan.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{stan\_data\_growth }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{N =} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(d\_growth),}
  \AttributeTok{y =} \FunctionTok{as.vector}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{log\_growth),}
  \AttributeTok{is\_evo   =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{is\_evo),}
  \AttributeTok{evo\_type =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{evo\_type),}
  \AttributeTok{Ci       =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Ci),}
  \AttributeTok{mat\_id   =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{mat\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{state\_id =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{state\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{use\_state\_anc =} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{use\_state     =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{B        =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{block\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{block\_id =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{block\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{K\_seq  =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{EE\_seq\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{seq\_id =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{EE\_seq\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{J\_rel      =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pop\_rel\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{pop\_rel\_id =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pop\_rel\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{J\_unrel      =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pop\_unrel\_id),}
  \AttributeTok{pop\_unrel\_id =} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(d\_growth}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pop\_unrel\_id)}
\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Here is stan code for just the full interaction model. This is new code
and has not yet replaced the old code with all the flags and switches.
We will set it up to be able to run and compare the total output.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{stan\_code\_growth\_interactionsonly }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"}


\StringTok{functions \{}
\StringTok{  // Center a vector so its elements sum to zero. Used to enforce sum{-}to{-}zero effects expressed}
\StringTok{  // as deviations from a baseline}
\StringTok{  vector center\_sum\_to\_zero(vector x) \{}
\StringTok{    return x {-} mean(x);}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{data \{}
\StringTok{  // Number of observations}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} N;}

\StringTok{  // log fitness, already transformed in data }
\StringTok{  vector[N] y;}

\StringTok{  // Indicator for whether an observation comes from an evolved population}
\StringTok{  // 0 = ancestral, 1 = evolved}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=1\textgreater{} is\_evo;}

\StringTok{  // Type of evolved treatment}
\StringTok{  // 0 = ancestral }
\StringTok{  // 1 = reliable evolved}
\StringTok{  // 2 = unreliable evolved}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=2\textgreater{} evo\_type;}

\StringTok{  // State index for each observation}
\StringTok{  // Full interaction model uses 8 states that combine blue light cue and maternal/grandmaternal oxygen environment.}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=8\textgreater{} state\_id;}

\StringTok{  // Number of assay blocks}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} B;}

\StringTok{  // Block identity for each observation}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=B\textgreater{} block\_id;}

\StringTok{  // Number of environmental sequences used for evolved treatments}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} K\_seq;}

\StringTok{  // Sequence identity for each observation}
\StringTok{  // We label the Ancestral rows can with seq\_id = 0 because they are not used.}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=K\_seq\textgreater{} seq\_id;}

\StringTok{  // Number of reliable replicate populations}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} J\_rel;}

\StringTok{  // Reliable population number, within reliable numbered form 1 to j}
\StringTok{  // all non{-}reliable rows are labeled with pop\_rel\_id = 0 because it won\textquotesingle{}t be used}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=J\_rel\textgreater{} pop\_rel\_id;}

\StringTok{  // Number of unreliable replicate populations}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} J\_unrel;}

\StringTok{  // Unreliable population number, within unreliable numbered form 1 to j}
\StringTok{  // all non{-}unreliable rows are labeled with pop\_unrel\_id = 0 because it won\textquotesingle{}t be used}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=J\_unrel\textgreater{} pop\_unrel\_id;}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{parameters \{}
\StringTok{  // Overall ancestral intercept}
\StringTok{  // This is the average ancestral log fitness before adding state effects}
\StringTok{  real alpha\_anc;}

\StringTok{  // Raw ancestral state effects for the 8 states}
\StringTok{  // These will later made to sum to zero and scaled by a sigma term{-}sigma\_state\_anc}
\StringTok{  vector[8] state\_raw\_anc;}

\StringTok{  // Standard deviation for ancestral state effects}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_state\_anc;}

\StringTok{  // Evolved{-}treatment shifts in intercept relative to the ancestor, relaible 1 unreliable 2}
\StringTok{  vector[2] delta\_alpha;}

\StringTok{  // treatment{-}specific deviations in state effects}
\StringTok{  // These will later made to sum to zero and scaled by a sigma term, relaible 1 unreliable 2}
\StringTok{  matrix[2, 8] delta\_state\_raw;}

\StringTok{  // Standard deviations for ancestral state effects, relaible 1 unreliable 2}
\StringTok{  vector\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{}[2] sigma\_delta\_state;}

\StringTok{  // Raw block effects, will be scaled and sum{-}to{-}zero. These apply to all observations in this block, regardless of experimental evolution treatment. }
\StringTok{  vector[B] z\_block;}

\StringTok{  // Standard deviation for block effects}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_block;}

\StringTok{  // Evolutionary sequence (order of A/N) effects. Only applies to evolved populations. }
\StringTok{  // additive model, applies to both Rel and Unrel with same parameter}
\StringTok{  // Will be sum{-}to{-}zero and scalled}
\StringTok{  vector[K\_seq] z\_seq;}

\StringTok{  // Standard deviation for sequence effects}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_seq;}

\StringTok{  // reliable population effects}
\StringTok{  // Will be sum{-}to{-}zero and scalled}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_rel] z\_pop\_rel;}

\StringTok{  // unreliable population effects}
\StringTok{  // Will be sum{-}to{-}zero and scalled}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_unrel] z\_pop\_unrel;}

\StringTok{  // standard deviation for replicate population effect}
\StringTok{  // This is shared between reliable and unreliable populations, but}
\StringTok{  // sum{-}to{-}zero acts within each evolutionary treatment. }
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_pop;}

\StringTok{  // standard deviation for the likelihood of observing each data point }
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_y;}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{transformed parameters \{}
\StringTok{  // ancestral state effects}
\StringTok{  // Apply sigma and sum to zero. }
\StringTok{  vector[8] state\_anc = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_state\_anc * state\_raw\_anc);}

\StringTok{  // Evolutionary treatment state effects{-} Reliable, Unreliable}
\StringTok{  // Multiply by the appropriate sigma\_delta and then enforce sum{-}to{-}zero}
\StringTok{  matrix[2, 8] delta\_state;}
\StringTok{  for (t in 1:2) \{}
\StringTok{    delta\_state[t] =}
\StringTok{      to\_row\_vector(center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_delta\_state[t] * to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw[t])));}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  // block effects, apply sigma and sum{-}to{-}zero}
\StringTok{  vector[B] block\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_block * z\_block);}

\StringTok{  // Sequence effects, multiply by sigma and sum{-}to{-}zero}
\StringTok{ vector[K\_seq] seq\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_seq * z\_seq);}

\StringTok{  // Reliable population effects, multiply by sigma and sum{-}to{-}zero}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_rel] pop\_rel\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_pop * z\_pop\_rel);}

\StringTok{  // Unreliable population effects, multiply by sigma and sum{-}to{-}zero}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_unrel] pop\_unrel\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_pop * z\_pop\_unrel);}

\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{model \{}
\StringTok{  // Prior for ancestral intercept}
\StringTok{  alpha\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1.5);}

\StringTok{  // Priors for ancestral state effects}
\StringTok{  // Raw effects have standard normal prior}
\StringTok{  // Their total scale is controlled by sigma\_state\_anc}
\StringTok{  state\_raw\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_state\_anc \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  // Priors for treatment{-}specific intercept shifts, quite broad but still regularizing}
\StringTok{  delta\_alpha \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}

\StringTok{  // Priors for treatment{-}specific state deviations}
\StringTok{  // Raw deviations are standard normal}
\StringTok{  // Their magnitudes are controlled by sigma\_delta\_state, this is common between}
\StringTok{  // Rel and Unrel, but unique from Ancestral.}
\StringTok{  to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw) \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_delta\_state \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  // Priors for block  effects}
\StringTok{  z\_block \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_block \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  // Priors for sequence  effects}
\StringTok{    z\_seq \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{    sigma\_seq \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  // Priors for replicate population effects}
\StringTok{    z\_pop\_rel \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{    z\_pop\_unrel \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  }
\StringTok{  // Shared prior scale for replicate population effects}
\StringTok{  sigma\_pop \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  // Prior for normal likelihood standard deviation}
\StringTok{  sigma\_y \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  // Likelihood starts here}
\StringTok{  for (n in 1:N) \{}
\StringTok{    // divide into fixed and non{-}fixed effects}
\StringTok{    real mu\_fixed;}

\StringTok{    // other contributions, labelled as epsilons in print version}
\StringTok{    real re\_block;}
\StringTok{    real re\_seq;}
\StringTok{    real re\_pop;}

\StringTok{    // For ancestral observations:}
\StringTok{    // mu = ancestral intercept + ancestral state effect}
\StringTok{    if (is\_evo[n] == 0) \{}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed = alpha\_anc + state\_anc[state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \} else \{}
\StringTok{      // For evolved observations we have to also include shift in intercept and shift in }
\StringTok{      // state{-}specific response.}
\StringTok{      int t = evo\_type[n];}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        (alpha\_anc + delta\_alpha[t]) +}
\StringTok{        (state\_anc[state\_id[n]] + delta\_state[t, state\_id[n]]);}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    // Block effect, each observation has one.}
\StringTok{    re\_block = block\_eff[block\_id[n]];}

\StringTok{    // set both the sequence and population specific effect variables at zero to start, }
\StringTok{    // if it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a specific effect for}
\StringTok{    // the current observation, it will add a 0 deviation to the mu value. }
\StringTok{    re\_seq = 0;}
\StringTok{    re\_pop = 0;}

\StringTok{    // if there is a sequence effect, add it now}
\StringTok{    if (seq\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_seq = seq\_eff[seq\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    if (pop\_rel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_rel\_eff[pop\_rel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    // If it is an Unreliable population, set the effect }
\StringTok{    if (pop\_unrel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_unrel\_eff[pop\_unrel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    // Calculate the likelhood as a sampling statemnet}
\StringTok{    // sum the effects to get the expected mean for observation }
\StringTok{    y[n] \textasciitilde{} normal(mu\_fixed + re\_block + re\_seq + re\_pop, sigma\_y);}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{  }
\StringTok{  }
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{generated quantities \{}
\StringTok{  // Pointwise log{-}likelihood values for model comparison}
\StringTok{  vector[N] log\_lik;}

\StringTok{  for (n in 1:N) \{}
\StringTok{    // Recompute the same linear predictor used in the model block}
\StringTok{    real mu\_fixed;}
\StringTok{    real re\_block;}
\StringTok{    real re\_seq;}
\StringTok{    real re\_pop;}
\StringTok{    real mu;}

\StringTok{    // Fixed effects for ancestral or evolved observations}
\StringTok{    if (is\_evo[n] == 0) \{}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed = alpha\_anc + state\_anc[state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \} else \{}
\StringTok{      int t = evo\_type[n];}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        (alpha\_anc + delta\_alpha[t]) +}
\StringTok{        (state\_anc[state\_id[n]] + delta\_state[t, state\_id[n]]);}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    // Block effect}
\StringTok{    re\_block = block\_eff[block\_id[n]];}

\StringTok{    // set both the sequence and population specific effect variables at zero to start, }
\StringTok{    // if it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a specific effect for}
\StringTok{    // the current observation, it will add a 0 deviation to the mu value. }
\StringTok{    re\_seq = 0;}
\StringTok{    re\_pop = 0;}

\StringTok{    // if there is a sequence effect, add it now}
\StringTok{    if (seq\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_seq = seq\_eff[seq\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    if (pop\_rel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_rel\_eff[pop\_rel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    // If it is an Unreliable population, set the effect }
\StringTok{    if (pop\_unrel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_unrel\_eff[pop\_unrel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    // sum the effects to get the expected mean for observation }
\StringTok{    mu = mu\_fixed + re\_block + re\_seq + re\_pop;}

\StringTok{    // Calculate log{-}likelihood }
\StringTok{    log\_lik[n] = normal\_lpdf(y[n] | mu, sigma\_y);}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{"}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{Setup code to compare models with/without additive and
interaction
effects}\label{setup-code-to-compare-models-withwithout-additive-and-interaction-effects}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{stan\_code\_growth\_full\_centered }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"}
\StringTok{functions \{}
\StringTok{  vector center\_sum\_to\_zero(vector x) \{}
\StringTok{    return x {-} mean(x);}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{data \{}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} N;}
\StringTok{  vector[N] y;}

\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=1\textgreater{} is\_evo;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=2\textgreater{} evo\_type;}

\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower={-}1, upper=1\textgreater{} Ci;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=4\textgreater{} mat\_id;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=8\textgreater{} state\_id;}

\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=0, upper=1\textgreater{} use\_state\_anc;}
\StringTok{  array[2] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=1\textgreater{} use\_state;}

\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} B;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=B\textgreater{} block\_id;}

\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} K\_seq;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=K\_seq\textgreater{} seq\_id;}

\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} J\_rel;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=J\_rel\textgreater{} pop\_rel\_id;}

\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} J\_unrel;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=J\_unrel\textgreater{} pop\_unrel\_id;}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{parameters \{}
\StringTok{  real alpha\_anc;}

\StringTok{  vector[4] mat\_raw\_anc;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_mat\_anc;}

\StringTok{  real beta\_cue\_anc;}

\StringTok{  vector[8] state\_raw\_anc;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_state\_anc;}

\StringTok{  vector[2] delta\_alpha;}

\StringTok{  matrix[2, 4] delta\_mat\_raw;}
\StringTok{  vector\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{}[2] sigma\_delta\_mat;}

\StringTok{  vector[2] delta\_beta\_cue;}

\StringTok{  matrix[2, 8] delta\_state\_raw;}
\StringTok{  vector\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{}[2] sigma\_delta\_state;}

\StringTok{  vector[B] z\_block;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_block;}

\StringTok{  vector[K\_seq] z\_seq;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_seq;}

\StringTok{  vector[J\_rel] z\_pop\_rel;}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_unrel] z\_pop\_unrel;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_pop;}

\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_y;}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{transformed parameters \{}
\StringTok{  vector[4] mat\_anc   = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_mat\_anc * mat\_raw\_anc);}
\StringTok{  vector[8] state\_anc = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_state\_anc * state\_raw\_anc);}

\StringTok{  matrix[2, 4] delta\_mat;}
\StringTok{  matrix[2, 8] delta\_state;}

\StringTok{  for (t in 1:2) \{}
\StringTok{    delta\_mat[t] = (center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_delta\_mat[t] * to\_vector(delta\_mat\_raw[t])))\textquotesingle{};}
\StringTok{    delta\_state[t] = (center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_delta\_state[t] * to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw[t])))\textquotesingle{};}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  vector[B] block\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_block * z\_block);}

\StringTok{  vector[K\_seq] seq\_eff;}
\StringTok{  if (K\_seq \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{    seq\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_seq * z\_seq);}

\StringTok{  vector[J\_rel] pop\_rel\_eff;}
\StringTok{  if (J\_rel \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{    pop\_rel\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_pop * z\_pop\_rel);}

\StringTok{  vector[J\_unrel] pop\_unrel\_eff;}
\StringTok{  if (J\_unrel \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{    pop\_unrel\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_pop * z\_pop\_unrel);}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{model \{}
\StringTok{  alpha\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1.5);}

\StringTok{  mat\_raw\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_mat\_anc \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  beta\_cue\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}

\StringTok{  state\_raw\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_state\_anc \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  delta\_alpha \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  to\_vector(delta\_mat\_raw) \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_delta\_mat \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  delta\_beta\_cue \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}

\StringTok{  to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw) \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_delta\_state \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  z\_block \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_block \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  if (K\_seq \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{    z\_seq \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{    sigma\_seq \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  if (J\_rel \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{    z\_pop\_rel \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}

\StringTok{  if (J\_unrel \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{    z\_pop\_unrel \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}

\StringTok{  sigma\_pop \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_y \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  for (n in 1:N) \{}
\StringTok{    real mu\_fixed;}

\StringTok{    if (is\_evo[n] == 0) \{}
\StringTok{      if (use\_state\_anc == 1) \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = alpha\_anc + state\_anc[state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{      \} else \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = alpha\_anc}
\StringTok{                 + mat\_anc[mat\_id[n]]}
\StringTok{                 + beta\_cue\_anc * Ci[n];}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \} else \{}
\StringTok{      int t = evo\_type[n];}

\StringTok{      if (use\_state[t] == 1) \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = (alpha\_anc + delta\_alpha[t])}
\StringTok{                 + (state\_anc[state\_id[n]] + delta\_state[t, state\_id[n]]);}
\StringTok{      \} else \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = (alpha\_anc + delta\_alpha[t])}
\StringTok{                 + (mat\_anc[mat\_id[n]] + delta\_mat[t, mat\_id[n]])}
\StringTok{                 + (beta\_cue\_anc + delta\_beta\_cue[t]) * Ci[n];}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    \{}
\StringTok{      real re\_block = block\_eff[block\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{      real re\_seq = 0;}
\StringTok{      real re\_pop = 0;}

\StringTok{      if (seq\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{        re\_seq = seq\_eff[seq\_id[n]];}

\StringTok{      if (pop\_rel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{        re\_pop += pop\_rel\_eff[pop\_rel\_id[n]];}

\StringTok{      if (pop\_unrel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{        re\_pop += pop\_unrel\_eff[pop\_unrel\_id[n]]; }

\StringTok{      y[n] \textasciitilde{} normal(mu\_fixed + re\_block + re\_seq + re\_pop, sigma\_y); // likelihood of data evaluation}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{generated quantities \{}
\StringTok{  vector[N] log\_lik;}

\StringTok{  for (n in 1:N) \{}
\StringTok{    real mu\_fixed;}

\StringTok{    if (is\_evo[n] == 0) \{}
\StringTok{      if (use\_state\_anc == 1) \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = alpha\_anc + state\_anc[state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{      \} else \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = alpha\_anc}
\StringTok{                 + mat\_anc[mat\_id[n]]}
\StringTok{                 + beta\_cue\_anc * Ci[n];}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \} else \{}
\StringTok{      int t = evo\_type[n];}

\StringTok{      if (use\_state[t] == 1) \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = (alpha\_anc + delta\_alpha[t])}
\StringTok{                 + (state\_anc[state\_id[n]] + delta\_state[t, state\_id[n]]);}
\StringTok{      \} else \{}
\StringTok{        mu\_fixed = (alpha\_anc + delta\_alpha[t])}
\StringTok{                 + (mat\_anc[mat\_id[n]] + delta\_mat[t, mat\_id[n]])}
\StringTok{                 + (beta\_cue\_anc + delta\_beta\_cue[t]) * Ci[n];}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    \{}
\StringTok{      real re\_block = block\_eff[block\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{      real re\_seq = 0;}
\StringTok{      real re\_pop = 0;}

\StringTok{      if (seq\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{        re\_seq = seq\_eff[seq\_id[n]];}

\StringTok{      if (pop\_rel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{        re\_pop += pop\_rel\_eff[pop\_rel\_id[n]];}

\StringTok{      if (pop\_unrel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0)}
\StringTok{        re\_pop += pop\_unrel\_eff[pop\_unrel\_id[n]];}

\StringTok{      log\_lik[n] = normal\_lpdf(y[n] | mu\_fixed + re\_block + re\_seq + re\_pop, sigma\_y);}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}
\StringTok{"}

\NormalTok{stan\_file\_growth\_full\_centered }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{write\_stan\_file}\NormalTok{(stan\_code\_growth\_full\_centered, }\AttributeTok{dir =} \StringTok{"stan\_cache"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}

\subsection{Model for the effect of evolutionary
sequence}\label{model-for-the-effect-of-evolutionary-sequence}

Added April 9, 2026

But actually do it for Unreliable too.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{stan\_code\_growth\_anc\_rel\_unrel\_by\_seq\_state\_only }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"}
\StringTok{functions \{}
\StringTok{  vector center\_sum\_to\_zero(vector x) \{}
\StringTok{    return x {-} mean(x);}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{data \{}
\StringTok{  // Number of observations}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} N;}

\StringTok{  // Observed log fitness}
\StringTok{  vector[N] y;}

\StringTok{  // 0 = Ancestral, 1 = Reliable, 2 = Unreliable}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=2\textgreater{} evo\_type;}

\StringTok{  // Full 8{-}state index}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=8\textgreater{} state\_id;}

\StringTok{  // Assay block}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} B;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=B\textgreater{} block\_id;}

\StringTok{  // Number of Reliable sequences}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} K\_seq\_rel;}

\StringTok{  // Number of Unreliable sequences}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} K\_seq\_unrel;}

\StringTok{  // Sequence ids for each observation}
\StringTok{  // Use 0 when sequence does not apply}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=K\_seq\_rel\textgreater{} seq\_id\_rel;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=K\_seq\_unrel\textgreater{} seq\_id\_unrel;}

\StringTok{  // Total number of Reliable replicate populations}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} J\_rel;}

\StringTok{  // Total number of Unreliable replicate populations}
\StringTok{  int\textless{}lower=1\textgreater{} J\_unrel;}

\StringTok{  // Population ids for each observation}
\StringTok{  // Use 0 when population effect does not apply}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=J\_rel\textgreater{} pop\_rel\_id;}
\StringTok{  array[N] int\textless{}lower=0, upper=J\_unrel\textgreater{} pop\_unrel\_id;}

\StringTok{  // Sequence membership of each Reliable population}
\StringTok{  array[J\_rel] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=K\_seq\_rel\textgreater{} pop\_seq\_of\_rel;}

\StringTok{  // Sequence membership of each Unreliable population}
\StringTok{  array[J\_unrel] int\textless{}lower=1, upper=K\_seq\_unrel\textgreater{} pop\_seq\_of\_unrel;}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{parameters \{}
\StringTok{  // Ancestral mean across states}
\StringTok{  real alpha\_anc;}

\StringTok{  // Ancestral state effects}
\StringTok{  vector[8] state\_raw\_anc;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_state\_anc;}

\StringTok{  // Reliable sequence{-}specific intercept shifts relative to Ancestral}
\StringTok{  vector[K\_seq\_rel] delta\_alpha\_rel\_seq;}

\StringTok{  // Reliable sequence{-}specific state deviations relative to Ancestral}
\StringTok{  matrix[K\_seq\_rel, 8] delta\_state\_raw\_rel\_seq;}
\StringTok{  vector\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{}[K\_seq\_rel] sigma\_delta\_state\_rel\_seq;}

\StringTok{  // Unreliable sequence{-}specific intercept shifts relative to Ancestral}
\StringTok{  vector[K\_seq\_unrel] delta\_alpha\_unrel\_seq;}

\StringTok{  // Unreliable sequence{-}specific state deviations relative to Ancestral}
\StringTok{  matrix[K\_seq\_unrel, 8] delta\_state\_raw\_unrel\_seq;}
\StringTok{  vector\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{}[K\_seq\_unrel] sigma\_delta\_state\_unrel\_seq;}

\StringTok{  // Block effects}
\StringTok{  vector[B] z\_block;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_block;}

\StringTok{  // Reliable replicate{-}population effects}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_rel] z\_pop\_rel;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_pop\_rel;}

\StringTok{  // Unreliable replicate{-}population effects}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_unrel] z\_pop\_unrel;}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_pop\_unrel;}

\StringTok{  // Residual standard deviation}
\StringTok{  real\textless{}lower=0\textgreater{} sigma\_y;}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{transformed parameters \{}
\StringTok{  vector[8] state\_anc = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_state\_anc * state\_raw\_anc);}

\StringTok{  matrix[K\_seq\_rel, 8] delta\_state\_rel\_seq;}
\StringTok{  matrix[K\_seq\_unrel, 8] delta\_state\_unrel\_seq;}

\StringTok{  vector[B] block\_eff = center\_sum\_to\_zero(sigma\_block * z\_block);}

\StringTok{  vector[J\_rel] pop\_rel\_eff;}
\StringTok{  vector[J\_unrel] pop\_unrel\_eff;}

\StringTok{  for (s in 1:K\_seq\_rel) \{}
\StringTok{    delta\_state\_rel\_seq[s] =}
\StringTok{      to\_row\_vector(}
\StringTok{        center\_sum\_to\_zero(}
\StringTok{          sigma\_delta\_state\_rel\_seq[s] * to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw\_rel\_seq[s])}
\StringTok{        )}
\StringTok{      );}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  for (s in 1:K\_seq\_unrel) \{}
\StringTok{    delta\_state\_unrel\_seq[s] =}
\StringTok{      to\_row\_vector(}
\StringTok{        center\_sum\_to\_zero(}
\StringTok{          sigma\_delta\_state\_unrel\_seq[s] * to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw\_unrel\_seq[s])}
\StringTok{        )}
\StringTok{      );}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  // Center Reliable population effects within sequence}
\StringTok{  for (s in 1:K\_seq\_rel) \{}
\StringTok{    int n\_in\_seq = 0;}
\StringTok{    real mean\_z = 0;}

\StringTok{    for (j in 1:J\_rel) \{}
\StringTok{      if (pop\_seq\_of\_rel[j] == s) \{}
\StringTok{        n\_in\_seq += 1;}
\StringTok{        mean\_z += z\_pop\_rel[j];}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    mean\_z /= n\_in\_seq;}

\StringTok{    for (j in 1:J\_rel) \{}
\StringTok{      if (pop\_seq\_of\_rel[j] == s) \{}
\StringTok{        pop\_rel\_eff[j] = sigma\_pop\_rel * (z\_pop\_rel[j] {-} mean\_z);}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  // Center Unreliable population effects within sequence}
\StringTok{  for (s in 1:K\_seq\_unrel) \{}
\StringTok{    int n\_in\_seq = 0;}
\StringTok{    real mean\_z = 0;}

\StringTok{    for (j in 1:J\_unrel) \{}
\StringTok{      if (pop\_seq\_of\_unrel[j] == s) \{}
\StringTok{        n\_in\_seq += 1;}
\StringTok{        mean\_z += z\_pop\_unrel[j];}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    mean\_z /= n\_in\_seq;}

\StringTok{    for (j in 1:J\_unrel) \{}
\StringTok{      if (pop\_seq\_of\_unrel[j] == s) \{}
\StringTok{        pop\_unrel\_eff[j] = sigma\_pop\_unrel * (z\_pop\_unrel[j] {-} mean\_z);}
\StringTok{      \}}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{model \{}
\StringTok{  alpha\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1.5);}

\StringTok{  state\_raw\_anc \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_state\_anc \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  delta\_alpha\_rel\_seq \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw\_rel\_seq) \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_delta\_state\_rel\_seq \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  delta\_alpha\_unrel\_seq \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  to\_vector(delta\_state\_raw\_unrel\_seq) \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_delta\_state\_unrel\_seq \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  z\_block \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_block \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  z\_pop\_rel \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_pop\_rel \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  z\_pop\_unrel \textasciitilde{} normal(0, 1);}
\StringTok{  sigma\_pop\_unrel \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  sigma\_y \textasciitilde{} exponential(1);}

\StringTok{  for (n in 1:N) \{}
\StringTok{    real mu\_fixed;}
\StringTok{    real re\_block;}
\StringTok{    real re\_pop;}

\StringTok{    if (evo\_type[n] == 0) \{}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \} else if (evo\_type[n] == 1) \{}
\StringTok{      int s = seq\_id\_rel[n];}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[state\_id[n]] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_alpha\_rel\_seq[s] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_state\_rel\_seq[s, state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \} else \{}
\StringTok{      int s = seq\_id\_unrel[n];}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[state\_id[n]] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_alpha\_unrel\_seq[s] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_state\_unrel\_seq[s, state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    re\_block = block\_eff[block\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    re\_pop = 0;}

\StringTok{    if (pop\_rel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_rel\_eff[pop\_rel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{    if (pop\_unrel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_unrel\_eff[pop\_unrel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    y[n] \textasciitilde{} normal(mu\_fixed + re\_block + re\_pop, sigma\_y);}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}

\StringTok{generated quantities \{}
\StringTok{  vector[N] log\_lik;}
\StringTok{  vector[8] mu\_anc\_state;}
\StringTok{  matrix[K\_seq\_rel, 8] mu\_rel\_state;}
\StringTok{  matrix[K\_seq\_unrel, 8] mu\_unrel\_state;}

\StringTok{  for (st in 1:8) \{}
\StringTok{    mu\_anc\_state[st] = alpha\_anc + state\_anc[st];}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  for (s in 1:K\_seq\_rel) \{}
\StringTok{    for (st in 1:8) \{}
\StringTok{      mu\_rel\_state[s, st] =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[st] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_alpha\_rel\_seq[s] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_state\_rel\_seq[s, st];}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  for (s in 1:K\_seq\_unrel) \{}
\StringTok{    for (st in 1:8) \{}
\StringTok{      mu\_unrel\_state[s, st] =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[st] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_alpha\_unrel\_seq[s] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_state\_unrel\_seq[s, st];}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{  \}}

\StringTok{  for (n in 1:N) \{}
\StringTok{    real mu\_fixed;}
\StringTok{    real re\_block;}
\StringTok{    real re\_pop;}
\StringTok{    real mu;}

\StringTok{    if (evo\_type[n] == 0) \{}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \} else if (evo\_type[n] == 1) \{}
\StringTok{      int s = seq\_id\_rel[n];}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[state\_id[n]] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_alpha\_rel\_seq[s] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_state\_rel\_seq[s, state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \} else \{}
\StringTok{      int s = seq\_id\_unrel[n];}
\StringTok{      mu\_fixed =}
\StringTok{        alpha\_anc +}
\StringTok{        state\_anc[state\_id[n]] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_alpha\_unrel\_seq[s] +}
\StringTok{        delta\_state\_unrel\_seq[s, state\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    re\_block = block\_eff[block\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    re\_pop = 0;}

\StringTok{    if (pop\_rel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_rel\_eff[pop\_rel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}
\StringTok{    if (pop\_unrel\_id[n] \textgreater{} 0) \{}
\StringTok{      re\_pop = pop\_unrel\_eff[pop\_unrel\_id[n]];}
\StringTok{    \}}

\StringTok{    mu = mu\_fixed + re\_block + re\_pop;}
\StringTok{    log\_lik[n] = normal\_lpdf(y[n] | mu, sigma\_y);}
\StringTok{  \}}
\StringTok{\}}
\StringTok{"}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
